33rd - 64th Decklists
=====================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX KUALA LUMPUR 2016](/en/events/coverage/gpkl16)
 on October 23, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











And because we know you want to see even more decklists, here is everyone else who had a money finish here at Grand Prix Kuala Lumpur. That's everybody from 33rd place to 64th place! What secrets can you uncover from within to prepare yourselves for the upcoming Standard tournaments?
